			BUI.ads.normalizeAdArray = function (actual) {
				'use strict';
				
				var newArray = new Array();
					
				for (var i = 0; i &lt; actual.length; i++) {
					if (actual[i]) {
						newArray.push(actual[i].toLowerCase().replace(/\s/g, '-'));
					}
				}
				
				return newArray;
			}

     $(function () {

		var relatedWidth = '938px'; // Default for 960 layout. Based on full 960 page width, minus 40px padding and 2px border.

		$("#video-meta-scroll").scrollbars();
		$("#video-meta-scroll-1200").scrollbars();

		// Set variable width for both break points.
		// NOTE: Seems hacky, but a specific value needs to be set by js when instantiating the related module.
		$(document.body).on('resize', function () {
			if (document.body.clientWidth &gt; 1400) {
				relatedWidth = '1178px';
			} else {
				// Restore default.
				relatedWidth = '938px';
			}

		});

		/********** Carousels **********/
			
			/*** Related Content Carousel ***/
			$("#related-content-cg").carouFredSel({
				responsive: true,
				width: "950px",
				circular: true,
				infinite: false,
				auto: false,
				items: {
					visible: function (num) {
						$("#related-content-cg-wrap").css({width: '100%'});
						$("#related-content").css({width: relatedWidth, overflow: "hidden"});
						return 5;

					width: 165,

	});
